 The Food Safety and Standards Authority of India (FSSAI) has filed a petition in the Supreme Court against the Bombay High Court order to lift ban on Maggi noodles in the country
 FSSAI ne ucch nyaayalay ke 13 agast ke aadesh ko ‘trutipurna’ qaraar dete hue sarkaar se sweekrut prayogshaalaon ko phir se pareekshan ke liye diye gayi namoonon kii shuchita par sawaal uthaaya he
 FSSAI has argued that instead of any neutral authority, the High Court has 'erred' by asking to provide new samples to Nestlé, the Indian arm of the Swiss company
 isse pehle, ucch nyaayalay ne desh main megi noodsl kii nau kismon par pratibandh lagane sambandhi bhartiya khaadya suraksha evam maanak praadhikaar or maharashtra ke khaadya niyantrak ke adeshon ko nirast kar diya tha
 The High Court had said that the principle of natural justice was not followed while imposing the ban as the party producing the magi was not heard
 FSSI sutron ne kaha ki yachika main khaadya niamak ke adhikariyon ke khilaaf kii gai pratikul tippaniyon ko bhi hataane kii maang kii gai he
 It states that the authority should be allowed to examine the samples in the laboratory under the relevant law and not to insist on testing only in government recognized laboratories which are very few in number
 ucch nyaayalay ne isse pehle FSSAI or maharashtra khaadya niamak epad ke aadesh ko nirast kar diya tha
 He banned nine varieties of Maggi noodles in the country

 Let's know the 5 symbols associated with Shiva and his glory
 rudraksh kaa arth he -rudra kaa aksh , mana jaataa he ki rudraksh kii utpatti bhagwaan shiv ke ashruon se hui he
 Rudraksha has been used as an ornament since ancient times, for protection, for planet peace and for spiritual benefit
 kul milakar mukhya rup se 17 prakaar ke rudraksh paae jate hai,parantu 12 mukhi rudraksh vishesh rup se prayog main aate hai
 Rudraksha can be worn on the wrist, throat and heart
 ise kanth pradesh tak dhaaran karnaa sarvottam hoga
 - Should wear twelve in the wrist, thirty-six in the throat and one hundred and eight donations on the heart
 - ek dana bhi dhaaran kar sakate hai par yah dana hryday tak hona chahie tathaa laal dhaage main hona chahie
 - You can wear Rudraksh on Chaturdashi of Krishna Paksha or on any Monday
 phalgun krishna chaturdashi arthath shivaratri ko rudraksh dhaaran karnaa sabase uttam hota he
 - Before wearing Rudraksha, he should dedicate it to Shiva and chant the mantra on the same rosary or Rudraksha- Those who wear Rudraksha should remain sattvic and keep the behavior pure otherwise Rudraksha will not be beneficial
 damru- bhagwaan shiv hi nrity or sangeet ke pravartak hai 
 - Shiva's damru not only has seven notes but also has an alphabet inside it
 - shiv ji kaa damru bajaanaa anand or mangal kaa dyotak he
 - They are happy to play Damru and also hear Damru
 - nity agar ghar main shiv stuti damru bajaakar kii jaay to ghar main kabhi amangal nahin hota
 Trident - be it any power of the world - physical, divine or physical, cannot stand in front of Shiva's trident
 - shiv kaa trishul har vyakti ko uske karm ke anusaar dand detaa he
 - For happiness and prosperity in the house, place or make a trident in the middle above the main door
 - trishul akruti tabhi dhaaran karen , jab aap kaa man,vachan or karm par purna niyantran ho
 Tripunda - Because of controlling the three qualities of Satoguna, Rajoguna and Tamoguna, Shiva uses Tripunda Tilak
 - yah tripund safed chandan kaa hota he 
 - Any person who is a devotee of Shiva can use Tripunda
 - tripund ke bich main laal rang kaa bindu , vishesh dashaon main hi lagaana chahie
 - The results of applying the tripund at the time of chanting meditation are very auspicious
 bhasma- bhagwaan shiv is duniya ke saare aakarshan se mukt hai
 - For him, this world, love and illusion, everything is nothing more than an ashes
 - sab kuch ek din bhasmeebhoot hokar samaapt ho jayega , bhasma isi baat kaa pratik he
 Shiva is also anointed with Bhasma , which leads to disinterest and enlightenment
